### Planner Response

Be look at the code configuration I just implemented, I have defined **12 Platform/System Modules** to be hidden from Business Users.

If you are seeing a difference of **8 modules** (89 vs 81), it implies that **4 of these modules** might not yet exist in your database or permission list, so they aren't affecting the count yet.

Here is the exact list of **12 Modules** that are configured to be **Hidden** for Business Users:

1.  **System**
2.  **Global**
3.  **Api Key**
4.  **Webhook**
5.  **Backup**
6.  **Audit Log**
7.  **Subscription**
8.  **Plugin**
9.  **Theme**
10. **License** (Newly added)
11. **Feature** (Newly added)
12. **Integration** (Newly added)

**Summary:**
*   **Total Hidden:** 12 Modules
*   **Your Observation:** 8 Modules difference
*   **Reason:** The last 3-4 modules (License, Feature, Integration) likely don't have generated permissions in your database yet, so they aren't appearing in the "Total" count to begin with.

So, for now, the effective difference is 8, but strictly speaking, it is **12 restricted modules**.

### Planner Response

Ami je code configuration ti implement korechi, shekhane mot **12ti Platform/System Modules** define kora hoyeche ja Business User-der theke **Hide (lukano)** thakbe.

Apni je **8ti module-er parthokko** dekhchen (89 vs 81), tar karon holo ei 12ti module-er moddhe **4ti module** somvoboto apnar database-e ekhono generate kora hoyni, tai egulo "Total" count-e ashche na.

Niche **12ti Hidden Module**-er list deya holo ja Business User-ra dekhte pabe na:

1.  **System**
2.  **Global**
3.  **Api Key**
4.  **Webhook**
5.  **Backup**
6.  **Audit Log**
7.  **Subscription**
8.  **Plugin**
9.  **Theme**
10. **License** (Notun add kora hoyeche)
11. **Feature** (Notun add kora hoyeche)
12. **Integration** (Notun add kora hoyeche)

**Summary:**
*   **Total Hidden:** 12ti Module.
*   **Apni dekhchen:** 8ti Module-er parthokko.
*   **Karon:** Baki 3-4ti module (License, Feature, Integration) hoyto ekhono apnar permission database-e nai, tai egulo gononay ashche na.

Tai technically ami **12ti system module block** korechi, kintu database-e currently active ache hoyto 8ti, tai apni 8tir parthokko dekhchen.

### User Input

ebar arekta poramorsho daw.. amr ekhane settings check korle dekhbe shob alada alada switch on/off korar option ace such as- pos/erp/crm/commerce. ekhon ami jodi emon kono userk emon resource-er permissions dei jei option ekhane on nei off. explain in bangla 

### Planner Response

Apnar upload kora chobi dekhechi. Eti ekti khub common ebong important architectural question.

Jodi settings-e **CRM, Commerce ba onno kono module OFF** thake, kintu apni user-ke sei module-er permission diye den, tahole **Best Practice** onusare nicher niomgulo mene chola uchit:

**1. Permission Dileo Kaj Hobe Na (Backend enforce korbe):**
User-er permission thaka sattwo, jodi system settings-e oi module **OFF** thake, tahole user oi page ba feature access korte parbe na.
*   **Logik:** Access = (User Permission âœ…) **AND** (Module Active âœ…).
*   Maney, duito condition-i TRUE hote hobe. Jekono ekta FALSE hole Access Denied hobe.

**2. User Create Korar Shomoy UI-te Hide Rakha (Frontend):**
Jodi settings-e *CRM* off thake, tahole User Create/Edit page-e permission list-e *CRM* related kono option dekhanoi uchit na.
*   **Keno?** Karon je feature-ti system-ei nai, tar permission deya user-er jonno irrelevant ebong confusing.
*   **Implementation:** [UserForm.tsx](cci:7://file:///e:/WEB-DEVELOPMENT/PROJECTS/Mern/signature-bangla/pos/signature-bangla-primary/signature-bangla-pos-frontend/src/components/modules/user-management/UserForm.tsx:0:0-0:0)-e amra jemon `PLATFORM_RESOURCES` filter korlam, thik temoni `activeModules` API theke ene, jegulo OFF ache, segulor resource-o list theke filter kore deya uchit.

**3. Jodi pore Module ON kora hoy?**
Jodi apni permission agei diye rakhen ebong pore Settings theke Module ON koren, tokhon user automaticaly access peye jabe.

**Amar Poramorsho (Suggestion):**
Settings-e OFF thaka module-gulor permission **User Form-e na dekhano**-i sobcheye bhalo UX (User Experience). Eti user-ke "Dead Permission" deya theke biroto rakhe.

Apni jodi chan, amra [UserForm](cci:1://file:///e:/WEB-DEVELOPMENT/PROJECTS/Mern/signature-bangla/pos/signature-bangla-primary/signature-bangla-pos-frontend/src/components/modules/user-management/UserForm.tsx:35:0-721:1)-e ei filtering logic-ti add korte pari, jate Settings-e OFF thaka module-gulo permission list-e na ashe. Janaben ki?

### User Input

ekhon tab ki shobguloii thakbe? 

### Planner Response

Ji, **shob tab-i thakbe**.

Settings page-e gele upore **General**, **Modules & Licensing**, **Appearance**, **Profile** - ei charti tab-i dekhte paben.

*   Sidebar theke "General Settings"-e click korle **General** tab open hobe.
*   Sidebar theke "Module Toggles"-e click korle **Modules** tab open hobe.

Tab gulo thakar karone apni "General" e dhukeo iccha korle click kore sohojei "Modules" ba onno settings e jete parben. Ei pattern tai holo standard.

Apni ki chan j settings-e dhukle onno tab gulo *lukiye* thakuk? (Usually seta user-friendly hoy na).

### Planner Response

**ChatGPT-er Poramorsho Ekdom Thik & Professional.**
Ami ChatGPT-er sathe 100% ekmot. O jeta boleche sheta **SaaS/Enterprise Software Architecture**-er standard practice.

**Why it is correct:**
1.  **Separation of Concerns:** "Malik/Shareholder" ra Governance (Decision making) part, ar "Staff/Manager" ra Operational (Daily kaj) part. Duto mix korle software messy hoye jay.
2.  **Security:** Shareholder-der sensitivity (Investment, % Ownership) ar Staff-der daily attendance ek jaygay thaka uchit na.

---

### Apnar Prosner Uttor:
**"Project-e malik pokkho/shareholder/invistor/staffder chuti and others shob add kora jabe??"**

**Uttyor**: **Haa, obosshoi jabe.** Tobe segulo alada alada Module-e thakbe.

#### 1. Staff Leave & Attendance (HRM Module)
Apnar codebase analyse kore dekhlam `RESOURCE_KEYS` e `STAFF`, `LEAVE`, `ATTENDANCE` already defined ache. So infrastructure ready.
*   **Location**: Sidebar > HRM (Human Resource Management)
*   **Users**: Managers & Staff.
*   **Operations**: Check-in, Leave Request, Payroll.

#### 2. Malik/Shareholder (Governance Module) (New Requirement)
Eta ChatGPT-er kotha moto amra ekta **"Governance"** ba **"Company Profile"** name-e module banabo.
*   **Location**: Sidebar > Company (Only for Owners).
*   **Users**: Owners & Investors.
*   **Operations**: View Reports, Manage Shares, Board Members.

---

**Next Step:**
Apni jodi chan, ami **"HRM Module"** (Leave/Attendance) ta sidebar-e enable kore dite pari, karon eta operational necessity.
Ar "Governance" part ta pore Phase-2 te kora jete pare jemon ChatGPT suggest koreche.

**Apni ki HRM Module (Leave/Attendance) enable korte chan?**

*Viewed [module-registry.ts](file:///e:/WEB-DEVELOPMENT/PROJECTS/Mern/signature-bangla/pos/signature-bangla-primary/signature-bangla-pos-frontend/src/config/module-registry.ts) *

### Planner Response

**Owner / Investor / Voting** feature niye amar recommendation holo:

Industrial Standard onujayi usually **Governance (Malik Pokkho)** aar **Operations (Staff/POS)** alada rakha hoy, karon requirements bhinno hoy. Tobe apni jodi ekta **"All-in-One Super App"** banate chan, tobe eta **same app-ei rakha somvob**, kintu kichu condition maintain korte hobe:

### Recommendation: **Same App but Strictly Separated Module**
Etake alada app na baniye, amra ekta natun Module create korte pari: **"Governance"** or **"Shareholder Management"**.

**Keno Same App-e Rakben? (Pros)**
1.  **Integrated Reports**: Investor-ra shorasori **Profit & Loss** report dekhte parbe (Real-time). Alada app hole data sync kora lagto.
2.  **Dividend Calculation**: Sales/Profit theke automatic share onujayi Dividend hisab kora jabe.
3.  **Cost Effective**: Alada maintain korte hobe na.

**Ki Ki Include Kora Jete Pare?**
1.  **Cap Table**: Kar koto % share ache.
2.  **Voting/Polls**: Guruttopurno decision-er jonno digital voting.
3.  **Documents**: Board Meeting Minutes, Legal Papers archive.
4.  **Dividend Payouts**: Profit distribution record.

**Jodi apni chan, amra `HRM` er moto `Governance` module add korte pari:**
*   Role: Only `Owner` / `Shareholder`. (Manager/Staff access pabe na).
*   Menu: `Governance` -> `Shareholders`, `Voting`, `Documents`.

**Apni ki `Governance` module ta implement korte chan?** Naki ekhon HRM/Payroll focus korben? HRM-e "Payroll" ta baki ache ja financials er sathe connected.

### Planner Response

**Feedback Implemented: 100% Alignment** âœ…

I have already implemented the changes requested in the previous step, so the design is now fully aligned with the "100% industrial-standard" feedback.

**Summary of what is done:**

1.  **SaaS Platform Visibility**: Removed from the **Company Creation Form**. Now only visible to Super Admins in System Settings.
2.  **Integrations Toggle**: Renamed to **"Integrations (Add-on)"** with description **"APIs, Webhooks & Gateways"** (Option B).
3.  **Governance Description**: Updated to **"Board-level management. Enable for Shareholder & Investor access."** to clarify it's for enterprise use.

**Next Step Proposal:**

The feedback mentioned:
> "Module â†’ Sidebar auto-mapping logic"

This refers to ensuring that the Sidebar **dynamically hides** menus if a module is disabled (e.g., if `ERP` is OFF, the `Inventory/Products` menu should vanish).

Currently, the sidebar is manually configured. **Shall I proceed with implementing the "Sidebar auto-mapping logic" now?**

```typescript
// Fixed block in group-manager.ts
allPermissions.forEach((p: any) => {
    const resourceName = p.resource as string;
    if (!resourceName) return;

    if (!permissionsByResource[resourceName]) {
        permissionsByResource[resourceName] = [];
    }

    const bucket = permissionsByResource[resourceName];
    if (bucket) {
        bucket.push(p._id as mongoose.Types.ObjectId);
    }
});
```

canShowMenu(item, user) {
  if (!hasPermission(item.permission)) return false;

  if (item.level === "platform" && user.role !== SUPER_ADMIN)
    return false;

  if (item.level === "company" && !user.companyId)
    return false;

  return true;
}
